Operational Rules 
The servers have the following rules. 
If you wish to participate in chat,
you MUST follow these rules. 
Violation of these rules can result in a
ban from the server (possibly permanent). 
1.Remember any rule can be 
  changed by Sega. 
2.NO IMPERSONATING, HARASSMENT,
  RACISM, SPOOFING, THREATS or 
  TAKEOVERS. 
3.Please don't type in all caps. 
  It's considered shouting and is 
  interpreted as rude. Please also 
  refrain from flooding or 
  spamming with text.
The following rules are designed to 
promote a user-friendly environment. 
1.Refrain from using all caps, use of
  bad language, use of improper or 
  inappropriate nicknames, discussions 
  dealing with sexual content, drugs, 
  references to drugs, adult oriented 
  topics, and racism. 
  Any violation of these rules will
  result in being banned.
